# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 01:13:22.389314

### Base Program

```py
def count_digit(d, low, high):
    count = 0
    for i in range(low, high + 1):
        num = i
        while num > 0:
            if num % 10 == d:
                count += 1
            num //= 10
    return count
```

### Input

```json
[95, 59, 67]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def count_digit(d, low, high):
    count = 0
    for i in range(low, high + 1):
        num = i
        while num > 0:
            if num % 10 == d:
                count += 1
            num //= 10
    return count
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

Message: 
```
Success
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def count_digit(var_0, var_1, var_2):
    count = 0
    for i in range(var_1, var_2 + 1):
        num = i
        while num > 0:
            if num % 10 == var_0:
                count += 1
            num //= 10
    return count
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def count_digit(d, low, high):
    count = 0
    for i in range(low, 1 + high):
        num = i
        while num > 0:
            if num % 10 == d:
                count += 1
            num //= 10
    return count
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def count_digit(var_3, var_4, var_5):
    count = 0
    for i in range(var_4, 1 + var_5):
        num = i
        while num > 0:
            if num % 10 == var_3:
                count += 1
            num //= 10
    return count
```
